<p itemprop="description">
Jack Sparrow races to recover the heart of Davy Jones to avoid enslaving his soul to Jones' service, as other friends and foes seek the heart for their own agenda as well.</p>

<h2>Storyline</h2>
<div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
<p>
Once again we're plunged into the world of sword fights and "savvy" pirates. Captain Jack Sparrow is reminded he owes a debt to Davy Jones, who captains the flying Dutchman, a ghostly ship, with a crew from hell. Facing the "locker" Jack must find the heart of Davy Jones but to save himself he must get the help of quick-witted Will Turner and Elizabeth Swan. If that's not complicated enough, Will and Elizabeth are sentenced to hang, unless will can get Lord Cutler Beckett Jack's compass, Will is forced to join another crazy adventure with Jack.                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=kate+Archie&amp;view=simple&amp;sort=alpha&amp;ref_=tt_stry_pl">kate Archie</a></em> </p>
</div>
<span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/title/tt0383574/plotsummary?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Plot Summary</a>
<span>|</span>
<a href="/title/tt0383574/synopsis?ref_=tt_stry_pl">Plot Synopsis</a>
</span>

<h2>Did You Know?</h2>
<div class="txt-block" id="trivia">
<h4>Trivia</h4>


The Dutch audience awarded it with the 'TV Krant Filmposter Award' of 2006.        <a class="nobr" href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv">See more</a>  
    </div>
<hr/>
<div class="txt-block" id="goofs">
<h4>Goofs</h4>
Monkey Jack was cured from the curse of immortality together with the rest of the crew at the climax of <a href="/title/tt0325980/">Fluch der Karibik</a>. However, in the post-credits scene of that movie, the monkey takes a coin, therefore making himself immortal again for <a href="/title/tt0383574/">Pirates of the Caribbean - Fluch der Karibik 2</a>.        <a class="nobr" href="trivia?tab=gf&amp;ref_=tt_trv_gf">See more</a>  
    </div>

<div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
<h2>User Reviews</h2>
<div class="user-comments">
<div class="tinystarbar" title="9/10">
<div style="width: 90px;"></div>
</div>
<span itemprop="review" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
<strong itemprop="name">pirates 2 not as 'sugar coated'!!!</strong>
<span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
<meta content="1" itemprop="worstRating"/>
<meta content="9" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
<meta content="10" itemprop="bestRating"/>
</span>
<div class="comment-meta">
                        5 July 2006 | by <a href="/user/ur4523661/?ref_=tt_urv"><span itemprop="author">blackpearl871</span></a>
<meta content="2006-07-05" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                              (Australia)
                         <a href="/user/ur4523661/comments?ref_=tt_urv">See all my reviews</a>
</div>
<div>
<p itemprop="reviewBody">When watching pirates 2 for the first time, you start to wonder what was going through director Gore Verbinski's mind. Pirates 2 shows a very different side to piracy than that of 'the curse of the black pearl'.<br/><br/>Disloyalty, greed and lying are the basic themes of piracy, but this has shown more in the second film than the first. Mr Verbinski has definitely shown a new side to piracy, making it not as 'sugar coated' as the first movie.<br/><br/>But overall, at the end you are still hanging of the end of your set as expected. Well done to all those involved. Pirates of the Caribbean: Dead man's chest was tops!!!!</p>
</div>
</span>
<hr/>
